# Event to Inherit
country_event = {
	id = 11101
	title = "EVTNAME11101"
	desc = "EVTDESC11101"
	picture = "Celebration"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA11101"
		FROM = {
			inherit = THIS
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 57094
	title = "CapSupply_Depot_EvtName"
	desc = "CapSupply_Depot_EvtDesc"
	picture = "Invention"


	trigger = {
		OR = {
			capital_scope = {
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = capital_supply_depot_pmodifier }
			}
			any_owned_province = {
				is_capital = no
				has_province_modifier = capital_supply_depot_pmodifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "CapSupply_Depot_EvtOptA"
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = no
				has_province_modifier = capital_supply_depot_pmodifier
			}
			remove_province_modifier = capital_supply_depot_pmodifier
		}
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = { name = capital_supply_depot_pmodifier duration = -1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 111011928
	title = "EVTNAME111011928"
	desc = "EVTDESC111011928"
	picture = "Celebration"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA111011928"
		FROM = {
			inherit = THIS
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB111011928"
		prestige = 1
		relation = {
			who = FROM
			value = -100
		}
		any_pop = {
			militancy = 3
			consciousness = 2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				NOT = {
					relation = { who = FROM value = 100 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

 OR = {

			 invention = capital_for_investors
		 }
 EGY = {
			 invention = capital_for_investors
		 }		
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 70

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9 
			average_consciousness = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9 
			average_consciousness = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9 
			average_consciousness = 7
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA100000"

			factor = 50
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB100000"

		}
	}

province_event = {
	id = 2020
	title = "EVTNAME2020"
	desc = "EVTDESC2020"
	picture = "ZULU"
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_colonial = no
		owner = {
			civilized = yes
			NOT = {
				religious_policy = moralism
				citizenship_policy = residency
				plurality = 100
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = {
				citizenship_policy = full_citizenship
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = {
				plurality = 20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = {
				plurality = 25
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = {
				plurality = 30
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA2020"
		any_pop = {
			militancy = 1
		}
		owner = {
			plurality = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB2020"
		any_pop = {
			militancy = -2
		}
		owner = {
			plurality = -1
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = 2070
	title = "EVTNAME2070"
	desc = "EVTDESC2070"
	picture = "VALLEYOFTHEKINGS"
	is_triggered_only = no

	trigger = {
		has_national_minority = yes
		has_recent_imigration = 30
		is_colonial = no
		owner = {
			citizenship_policy = full_citizenship
			NOT = {
				plurality = 100
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			NOT = {
				average_militancy = 3
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			NOT = {
				average_consciousness = 4
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					plurality = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA2070"
		state_scope = {
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_culture = no
					is_accepted_culture = no
				}
				militancy = -1
			}
		}
		THIS = {
			plurality = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 19501
	title = "EVTNAME19501"
	desc = "EVTDESC19501"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC19501_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC19501_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC19501_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "GOLDRUSH"
	
	trigger = {
		is_greater_power = yes
		any_neighbor_country = {
			has_country_modifier = witwatersrand_gold_rush
			is_greater_power = no
			NOT = {
				num_of_cities = 10
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA19501"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = witwatersrand_gold_rush
			}
			add_casus_belli = {
				target = THIS
				type = conquest
			}
			remove_country_modifier = witwatersrand_gold_rush
		}
	}
}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { involved_in_crisis = yes }

		OR = {
			constructing_cb_type = acquire_state
			constructing_cb_type = conquest
			constructing_cb_type = demand_concession_casus_belli
			constructing_cb_type = establish_protectorate_casus_belli
			}
		NOT = {
			OR = {	
					has_country_modifier = CB_gen_plus
					has_country_modifier = CB_gen_minus
				}
			}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			press_rights = state_press
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			press_rights = censored_press
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			press_rights = free_press
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA90000"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = CB_gen_plus
			duration = 50
		}
	}
}

# Valley of The Kings
country_event = {
	id = 19040
	title = "EVTNAME19040"
	desc = "EVTDESC19040"
	picture = "ValleyoftheKings"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA19040"
		set_global_flag = egyptian_excavation_rights
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id=19041 days=0 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_global_flag = egyptian_excavation_rights
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = {
					prestige = 65
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = {
					is_greater_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB19040"
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id=19042 days=0 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	id = 23402 

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = Host1Olympiad }
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = GRENoHost1Olympiad
			NOT = { exists = GRE }
		}
		has_country_flag = IOCMember
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = Host1Olympiad
				has_country_flag = Attend1Olympiad
				has_country_flag = NoHost1Olympiad
			}
		}
		year = 1895
		NOT = { year = 1898 }
	}
 
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			year = 1896
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			year = 1897
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			rank = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			rank = 8
		}
	}

	title = "EVTNAME23401"
	desc = "EVTDESC23402"
	picture = "Olympics"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA23401" # Send invites to other IOC members
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = IOCMember
			}
			relation = {
				who = THIS
				value = 25
			}
		}
		prestige = 10
		set_global_flag = Host1Olympiad
		set_country_flag = Host1Olympiad
		set_country_flag = Attend1Olympiad
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB23401" # NOT interested
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = IOCMember
			}
			relation = {
				who = THIS
				value = -25
			}
		}
		prestige = -10
		set_country_flag = NoHost1Olympiad
	}
}

	id = 23403 # Attend 1896 Olympics 

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = Host1Olympiad
		has_country_flag = IOCMember
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = Attend1Olympiad
				has_global_flag = Hold1Olympiad
			}
		}
		year = 1895
		NOT = { year = 1898 }
	}
 
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			year = 1896
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			year = 1897
		}
	}

	title = "EVTNAME23403"
	desc = "EVTDESC23403"
	picture = "Olympics"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA23403" # Send a delegation to the games
		prestige = 10
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = IOCMember
			}
			relation = {
				who = THIS
				value = 25
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = Attend1Olympiad
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB23403" # We're NOT going this year
		prestige = -10
		any_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = IOCMember
			}
			relation = {
				who = THIS
				value = -25
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NoAttend1Olympiad
	}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			NOT = {
				average_militancy = 5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			poor_strata_life_needs = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			poor_strata_everyday_needs = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			liberal = 30
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA190"
		remove_country_modifier = temperance_league
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_province_modifier = beer_halls
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = beer_halls
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB190"
		random_state = {
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 3
					ideology = liberal
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	trigger = {
		year = 1849
		not = { year = 1935 }
		not = { has_global_flag = PlanRegionalFair }
		not = { has_country_flag = regionalfairplanner }
		civilized = yes
		or = { 
			industrial_score = 50 # limit to major non-western economies if not a GP
			and = {
				is_greater_power = yes # nation is a great power

			}
		}
